            Multi-Screen Connect
          </p> <p class="sub-1" data-v-55483450="">Work across your phone, tablet, and PC seamlessly</p> <p class="sub-2" data-v-55483450="">
            Cross-device communication | app relay | file transfer | file editing | clipboard sync
          </p></div> <div id="downloadButton" class="download-button pc-hover" data-v-55483450="">
          Download
        </div></section> <main class="mainContainer" data-v-55483450=""><div class="content full-content notChinese" data-v-55483450=""><div class="text-wrap" data-v-55483450=""><div class="text first out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Connect when near
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Sign in to the same account on your phone, tablet, and computer. Your phone will automatically connect to your tablet or computer when they are near each other, allowing you to perform tasks across devices.
You can also manually connect to your phone on your tablet or computer.
              </p> <p class="desc-two" data-v-55483450="">
                *To use this feature, update your phone and tablet to ColorOS 13.1 or a later version and Multi-Screen Connect on your computer to PC_Connect_3.3.5.0070 or a later version.
              </p></div> <div class="text two out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                App relay
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                You can use an app on your phone, and then switch to your computer or tablet and pick up where you left off. Switching from your tablet to your phone is also supported.
              </p> <p class="desc2" data-v-55483450="">
                *To use this feature, update your phone and tablet to ColorOS 13.1 or a later version and Multi-Screen Connect on your computer to PC_Connect_3.3.5.0070 or a later version.
              </p></div> <div class="text sixth out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Open multiple apps at the same time
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Multitask with up to 3 phone apps on your PC. One for finding travel recommendations, another for making bookings, doubling your efficiency.
              </p> <p class="desc2" data-v-55483450="">
                *Supports devices running ColorOS 12.1 or later versions.
              </p></div> <div class="text second out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">Edit files across devices</p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Drag and drop to transfer files from one device to another. Open a file on your phone directly from your PC to edit it and save it to your computer.
              </p></div> <div class="text third out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Sync clipboard
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Your PC clipboard is also synced with your phone. Simply copy text from your phone and paste it to your PC.
              </p></div> <div class="text forth out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Sync notifications <br data-v-55483450=""></p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                View and process text messages and app notifications straight from your PC.
              </p></div> <div class="text sevenOne out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Communication sharing
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Share your phone's communication functions with a nearby device so you can make and receive phone calls, send and receive messages, and access the internet on that device.
              </p> <p class="desc2" data-v-55483450="">
                Remarks: <br data-v-55483450="">
                1. Any fees incurred when using this feature will be charged to your phone. <br data-v-55483450="">
                2. Communication sharing relies on the connection between phones and tablets and is only supported by specific devices running ColorOS 13.1 or a later version. Visit OPPO Community to learn about supported devices and the ColorOS Upgrade Plan. <br data-v-55483450=""></p></div> <div class="text seventh out" data-v-55483450=""><p class="title" data-v-55483450="">
                Make calls across devices
              </p> <p class="desc" data-v-55483450="">
                Make and receive phone calls on your PC, and switch between PC and phone audio output.
              </p> <div class="desc2" data-v-55483450="">
                Remarks: <br data-v-55483450="">
                1. To use this feature, update your phone and tablet to ColorOS 13.0 or a later version and Multi-Screen Connect on your computer to PC_Connect_3.3.5.0070 or a later version. <br data-v-55483450="">
                2. Only the OPPO's Phone app supports cross-device call notifications.
                <span style="cursor: pointer;display:inline-block;color: #007BFF;" data-v-55483450="">
                  (Supported models) </span>
                <br data-v-55483450="">
                3. Cross-device phone call experiences may vary when you use third-party apps. <br data-v-55483450="">
                4. If your device is equipped with a Realtek sound card, we recommend turning on Acoustic Echo Cancellation (AEC) for a better audio experience. 

                <span style="cursor: pointer;display:inline-block;color: #007BFF;" data-v-55483450="">
                  (Click to learn how) </span>

                Take a photo or screenshot on your phone and view it on your PC. You can also copy or save the image or simply drag it to a program on your PC for use.

          3. The screencast image quality and the file transfer speed may be affected by signal interference from other nearby devices.<br data-v-26d6929b="">

          How to turn on Acoustic Echo Cancellation (AEC)?
        </div></div> <div class="echo-content-container" data-v-55483450=""><div data-v-55483450="">
          1.Confirm your PC uses a Realtek sound card: <br data-v-55483450="">
          Right-click This PC - Manage - Device Manager - Sound, video, and game controllers to see if there is Realtek sound card information.
        </div> <div data-v-55483450="">2. If your device uses a Realtek sound card, turn on Acoustic Echo Cancellation (AEC) in the Microphone Effects tab of Realtek Audio Console.</div> <div data-v-55483450="">3.You may download Realtek Audio Console from its official site if you can't find it on your PC.</div></div></div></div></div> <!----> <div class="ie-toast-container" style="display:none;" data-v-e7b325c8="">
